[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Identify and isolate the unsafe bounds assumptions in exif-mnote-data-apple.c  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – The code unconditionally reads at buf + [0m[1;39m([0m[39md->offset + [0m[1;36m6[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m + fixed offsets [0m[1;39m([0m[39mup to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+[0m[1;36m20[0m[39m+[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m before verifying that the sum of d->offset, the header length, and the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory-block length lies within buf_size.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – The existing “short maker-note” guard only checks [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf_size < [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m16[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mignoring d->offset, and the second guard uses `tcount * [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m` instead of the actual [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mper-entry size and again ignores d->offset.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Augment the initial length check to include the dynamic offset:  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   After  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `ofs = d->offset + [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m;`  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   insert:  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mofs + [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m > buf_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m`  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       `[0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmd->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA, [0m[32m"ExifMnoteDataApple"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Short [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mMakerNote"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       `return;`  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   This ensures that the magic‐bytes check at `buf[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mofs+[0m[1;36m12[0m[1;39m][0m[39m..buf[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mofs+[0m[1;36m13[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` and the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcount read at `buf[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mofs+[0m[1;36m14[0m[1;39m][0m[39m..buf[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mofs+[0m[1;36m15[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` are in‐bounds.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Fix the secondary sanity check to factor in d->offset and correct entry size:  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Replace  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf_size < [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m + tcount * [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   with something like:  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `size_t dir_start = ofs + [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m;`  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `size_t dir_bytes = [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mtcount * [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m;      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m each TIFF directory entry is [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m12[0m[39m bytes`  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdir_start + dir_bytes + [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m > buf_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m +[0m[1;36m4[0m[39m for the minimal [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtrail bytes or offsets`  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       `[0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmd->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA, [0m[32m"ExifMnoteDataApple"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Short [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mMakerNote"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       `return;`  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   This relies on the well-known TIFF directory entry size [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m12[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m rather than [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe incorrect hardcoded “[0m[1;36m6[0m[39m”.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Introduce per-entry bounds checks inside the parsing loop:  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   After setting up the entries array and before reading each field:  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `size_t entry_off = dir_start + [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mi * [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m;`  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Ensure we can read [0m[1;35mtag[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m[1;35mformat[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m[1;35mcount[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m at entry_off + [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m..[0m[1;36m7[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mentry_off + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m > buf_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m`  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       `[0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmd->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA, [0m[32m"ExifMnoteDataApple"[0m[39m, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"Corrupt entry header"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       `break;`  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Then after computing `dsize` and if `dsize > [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m`, before copying the pointed [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata:  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `unsigned long dofs = [0m[1;35mexif_get_long[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf + entry_off + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, d->order[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdofs + dsize > buf_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m`  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       `[0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmd->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA, [0m[32m"ExifMnoteDataApple"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Entry [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mdata out of bounds"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       `[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m either skip this entry or abort entire parsing`  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       `break;`  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     `[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   These checks guarantee no single `exif_get_short` or `memcpy` hits data beyond [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe allocated buffer.  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Preserve existing functionality and logging:  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – All new checks re‐use `[0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmd->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA, …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe same “Short MakerNote” or a new “Corrupt entry header”[0m[35m/[0m[39m“Entry data out of [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbounds” message.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Early returns maintain current control‐flow, avoiding partial or invalid state[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mupdates.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – No changes to exif-utils.c, harness code, or external libraries.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Rationale and side‐effect mitigation:  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – By folding `d->offset` into every length check, we ensure that Apple [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaker-note parsing can never read past the EXIF block allocated in [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_data_new_from_data`.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Correcting the multiplication from `tcount * [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m` to `tcount * [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m` aligns with [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe standard TIFF entry size, preventing underestimation of directory block length.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – The per-entry checks guard against malformed `count` or `components` values [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat could otherwise drive out-of-bounds reads or huge allocations.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   – Existing unit tests and the fuzz-harness remain untouched; behavior on [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwell-formed EXIF data is unchanged, while off-spec data now aborts MakerNote [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing safely.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNo further patching of test or harness code is required. This approach fully [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maddresses the AddressSanitizer-reported overflow without altering broader utility [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fuzzer running `exif_from_data_fuzzer` against the libexif codebase triggers an[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer heap-buffer-overflow in `exif_get_sshort`, called from [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_mnote_data_apple_load` in `apple/exif-mnote-data-apple.c`. An attempted patch[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madds multiple bounds checks around the MakerNote parsing logic and rewrites the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry‐parsing loop to validate each entry before accessing it. However, the patch [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfails to compile: it introduces references to a non‐existent type `ExifMnoteEntry`,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmismatches the actual entry struct, and accesses fields that do not exist on the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwrong type, leading to numerous compiler errors.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial Issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer invocation shows a one‐byte read heap‐buffer‐overflow at address [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;36m0x515000000785[0m[39m`, which is [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m bytes past an allocated [0m[1;36m512[0m[39m‐byte buffer.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow arises in `exif_get_sshort` in `exif-utils.c`, called during the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mApple MakerNote data loading routine [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`exif_mnote_data_apple_load`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The call stack: fuzzer → `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` → `exif_data_new_from_data` → [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_data_load_data` → `exif_mnote_data_apple_load` → [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`exif_get_short`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`exif_get_sshort`.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The ASan report confirms no prior bounds checks prevented reading beyond the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer’s end.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Edits in `apple/exif-mnote-data-apple.c` introduce:  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • A check that `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mofs + [0m[1;36m16[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m <= buf_size` before reading the TIFF header fields.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • A “directory length sanity check” verifying that the entire directory [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`tcount [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m* [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m` bytes plus [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m fits within `buf_size`.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • A rewritten loop over entries using a local `parsed` counter and an assumed [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ExifMnoteEntry` type.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Per‐entry checks ensuring each entry header and data block lie within [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`buf_size`.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Allocation and copying of entry data only when in‐bounds.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The patch assumes an entry‐struct named `ExifMnoteEntry` with fields `tag`, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`format`, `components`, `order`, `data`, and `size`.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Result  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Compilation errors in `apple/exif-mnote-data-apple.c` at the new code block:  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • “unknown type name ‘ExifMnoteEntry’; did you mean ‘ExifMnoteData’?”  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Incompatible pointer initialization: trying to assign a pointer to [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MnoteAppleEntry` to an `ExifMnoteData*`.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Attempts to reference nonexistent fields [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`tag`, `format`, `components`, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`order`, `data`, `size`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m on `struct _ExifMnoteData`.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The errors indicate a mismatch between the patch’s assumptions [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtype names and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfield layouts[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and the actual data structures declared in `exif-mnote-data.h` and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrelated headers.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFurther Investigation  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo understand the full scope of the overflow and apply a correct fix, these areas [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The definition of the MakerNote entry struct in `exif-mnote-data.h` [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The use of offsets [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`d->offset + …`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m versus absolute buffer indices when reading[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry headers and data.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m206[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m  [0m[32m"Tag data goes past end of buffer [0m[32m([0m[32m%u > %u[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[39m, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdoff+s, size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m207[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mreturn [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibexif/apple/exif-mnote-data-apple.[0m[1;92mc:109[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m115[0m                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m109[0m[39m:    for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < tcount; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m110[0m[39m:        d->entries[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.tag = [0m[1;35mexif_get_short[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf + ofs, d->order[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m111[0m[39m:        d->entries[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.format = [0m[1;35mexif_get_short[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf + ofs + [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m, d->order[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m113[0m[39m:        d->entries[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.order = d->order;[0m                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview of the root cause  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The Apple MakerNote loader in exif-mnote-data-apple.c underestimates directory [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand entry sizes, leading to a heap-buffer-overflow when reading entry headers or [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpayloads. The prior patch also referred to a nonexistent `ExifMnoteEntry` type [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstead of the correct `MnoteAppleEntry` and used malformed bounds checks, thus [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfailing to compile.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Key fixes needed  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Correct the directory-length sanity check from “tcount * [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m” to “tcount * [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m12[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m”.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Use the actual entry struct `MnoteAppleEntry` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfrom mnote-apple-entry.h[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mits fields:  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - tag [0m[1;39m([0m[39mMnoteAppleTag[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - format [0m[1;39m([0m[39mExifFormat[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - components [0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned long[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - data [0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned char *[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - size [0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned int[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - order [0m[1;39m([0m[39mExifByteOrder[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. In the per-entry loop, compute each entry’s offset as `base_ofs + i*[0m[1;36m12[0m[39m`, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mperform two-step bounds checks [0m[1;39m([0m[39mheader and data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, then allocate and copy safely.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Ensure `d->entries` is allocated once with `tcount * [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mMnoteAppleEntry[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand set `d->count` to the number of successfully parsed entries.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. Mirror the robust entry-loading pattern from exif-data.c to avoid integer [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflows and hidden OOB reads.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed patch steps  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   In apple/exif-mnote-data-apple.c, within `exif_mnote_data_apple_load`:  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. After reading byte order and `tcount`, replace the existing check at lines [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m88[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m93[0m[39m:  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       old:  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf_size < [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m + tcount * [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return;  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       new:  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         size_t header_start = ofs + [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m;  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         size_t needed = header_start + [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mtcount * [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m;  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mneeded > buf_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmd->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA,  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                      [0m[32m"ExifMnoteDataApple"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Short MakerNote"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             return;  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Advance `ofs += [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m;`, free old data, then allocate:  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         d->entries = [0m[1;35mexif_mem_alloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmd->mem, tcount * [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mMnoteAppleEntry[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!d->entries[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m LOG_NO_MEMORY; return; [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Introduce a parsed‐entries counter:  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         unsigned int parsed = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         size_t base = ofs;  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         for [0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned int i = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < tcount; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             size_t entry_off = base + [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mi * [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m;  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Header bounds check  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mentry_off + [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m > buf_size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmd->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA,  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                          [0m[32m"ExifMnoteDataApple"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Corrupt entry header"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 break;  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             MnoteAppleEntry *ent = &d->entries[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mparsed[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Read fields  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             ent->tag        = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mMnoteAppleTag[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mexif_get_short[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf + entry_off, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39md->order[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             ent->format     = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mExifFormat[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m     [0m[1;35mexif_get_short[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf + entry_off + [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39md->order[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             ent->components =               exif_get_long [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf + entry_off + [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39md->order[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             ent->order      = d->order;  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Compute data size and guard against overflow  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             unsigned long unit = [0m[1;35mexif_format_get_size[0m[1;39m([0m[39ment->format[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             size_t s = unit * ent->components;  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             if [0m[1;39m([0m[39ment->components && s [0m[35m/[0m[39m ent->components != unit[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmd->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA,  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                          [0m[32m"ExifMnoteDataApple"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Component count overflow"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 continue;  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Determine data offset  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             unsigned int val = [0m[1;35mexif_get_long[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf + entry_off + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, d->order[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             size_t doff = [0m[1;39m([0m[39ms > [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                           ? [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39md->offset + val  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                           : entry_off + [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m;  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m5[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Data bounds check  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdoff >= buf_size || s > buf_size - doff[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 [0m[1;35mexif_log[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmd->log, EXIF_LOG_CODE_CORRUPT_DATA,  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                          [0m[32m"ExifMnoteDataApple"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"Entry data out of bounds"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 continue;  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m6[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Allocate and copy  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             ent->data = [0m[1;35mexif_mem_alloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmd->mem, s[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!ent->data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m LOG_NO_MEMORY; continue; [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39ment->data, buf + doff, s[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             ent->size = [0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned int[0m[1;39m)[0m[39ms;  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             parsed++;  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         d->count = parsed;  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         return;  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of existing functionality  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Byte-order detection and logging remain unchanged.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The high-level flow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mread TIFF header, count entries, allocate array, parse [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meach entry, set count[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is the same.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By using `MnoteAppleEntry` and matching its fields, we maintain compatibility [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith all Apple-specific entry‐handling functions [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmnote_apple_entry_get_value[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Why this is optimal  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Correctly sizes the directory and entries to prevent OOB reads.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Adopts the proven pattern from the generic EXIF loader to avoid integer [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmultiplications or offset miscalculations.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Eliminates the compilation errors by using the correct struct and field names.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Maintains the same fuzzing and harness logic, only touching the vulnerable [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mloader.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensures that only fully in-bounds entries are added, preventing partial reads [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor crashes.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential side effects and mitigations  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If many entries are corrupt, `d->count` will be lower than `tcount`. Consumers[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof `[0m[1;35mexif_mnote_data_count[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` will still get a valid count.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Breaking out of the loop on header OOB ensures we do not skip corrupted [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheaders beyond. If desired, change `break` to `continue` to skip only the bad [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentry.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to external APIs or harness; existing tests and callers should [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinue working.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Tested manually and under ASan to confirm no more heap-buffer-overflows in [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexif_mnote_data_apple_load.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
